<Rating>5<//Rating>< Text>
A few years ago, I injured my back by bending and twisting down abruptly (without weight or load) and could not work for a few days and would have pain and spasms for weeks.  I eventually tried massage therapy, which only offered temporary relief, before being introduced to Dr. Sahota, whom introduced me to chiropractic care.  Chiropractic care focuses on a drug-free approach along with spine manipulation, traction, and core balancing and strength training.

I would see him three times a week, where he would adjust my spine, apply traction and use other tools / machines to loosen and maintain movement in my lower back, shoulders and neck.  He would then have me perform core balance and training exercises that he would also have me practice at home.  He would educate me on the the spine and muscles as well as what good habits to practice to prevent further deterioration.

Seeing Dr. Sahota has absolutely been life-changing and I am stronger, stand up straighter, and more pain-free than I have been in years.  I encourage anyone with back pain or problems to see him as he is thorough, educational, motivational, and genuinely cares about people's back pain.  Ask him about his motivation for becoming a chiropractor and you will know why he is passionate about people's spines.  He is great doctor and professional and you will be taken care of.</Text>

<UserId.>107234914374636956122</UserId.><Name>Michael Perez</Name>< Date>
1506472903817< /Date>
<Rating>5</Rating>< Review>
I can't say enough about the concept of combining culinary art, with the science of chemistry, that is really what baking is all about!

After all, it's Elemental! It's something that I Periodically think, while sitting at a table, especially when enjoying gourmet cookies!

So what better place to go than a high tech cookie laboratory, where they have a Periodic Table of Cookies!

They even got formulas written on the walls! You can even go in your lab coat, wear your safety goggles, and get your Science on, writing on your clipboard, taking copious detailed notes and diagrams, while observing them creating these culinary delights!

And the bottom line is the cookies are GOOD!!!

If it wasn't for that, all this would fall apart... because that's how the cookie crumbles.

Seriously, give it a try, you won't be disappointed!<//Review>

<user>111820199041013779119< /user></record></dataset><record>
<Time>1468830202815<//Time>< review>
Such a clever little cookie shop! We loved every cookie we tried but the chocolate chip is a MUST here. The BEST chocolate chip cookie we ever had!

Atmosphere: The inside is soo beautifully designed with different colors and textures that all go together in harmony. There are two larger tables in the middle and seating at the bar. The tables also have quality crafted basic games to enjoy such as tick tac toe. One of our favorite touches was the periodic table with cookie ingredients!

Food: The cookies are perfectly made, each one its own unique taste. A must try is the chocolate chip cookie, ice cream sandwich version!

Employees: All the employees were really nice and we even got a chance to talk to the owner who was the sweetest lady yet. We loved hearing her passion for this store and how she was inspired by her husband who is a scientist. What a cool story :)

You must go in and try it for yourself or order it at your next party.</review>

<userid>102590670193853476858<//userid>< Name>
Jo W<//Name>
<Time>1447881406653<//Time><Rating>5< /Rating>< text>
A cute, quaint little boutique bookstore in Rockridge. I've popped in here many times throughout high school to browse the selections. Over the years, they've updated the organization of the store--the children's section is much neater now. It used to be much messier and crowded. Lighting has brightened, and even though this is a pretty small bookstore, they still have a decent selection of books, and I can spend quite a while browsing here. They also have couches that you can sit on and read.

The staff is also very friendly and knowledgeable. Even if they don't have a book in their store, they're able to order it for you so that it's ready for you to pick up when it arrives. Definitely happy to see this local indie bookstore surviving the recession and remaining a staple in the Rockridge neighborhood.< /text>
